TITLE      Neutron activation cross sections measured at KRI      41614  1    3 
           in neutron energy region 13.4 - 14.9 MeV               41614  1    4 
AUTHOR     (A.A.Filatenkov)                                       41614  1    5 
INSTITUTE  (4RUSRI)                                               41614  1    6 
REFERENCE  (R,INDC(CCP)-0460,2016)                                41614  1    7 
REL-REF    (N,41298001,A.Filatenkov+,R,RI-252,1999)               41614  1    8 
           (N,41240001,A.Filatenkov+,R,RI-252,1999)               41614  1    9 
            Data from initial publication are in Entries          41614  1   10 
            41240 - for energy region 13.4-14.9 MeV,              41614  1   11 
            41298 - for 14.1 MeV .                                41614  1   12 
FACILITY   (CCW,4RUSRI)  Neutron Generator NG-400 .               41614  1   13 
           Voltage 220-320 kV, the deuteron current 0.01-0.5 mA . 41614  1   14 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) Ti-T target thickness 1-2 mg/cm2.                41614  1   15 
SAMPLE     The samples were gathered into assemblies that were    41614  1   16 
           mounted relative to the beam direction at the angles of41614  1   17 
           0, 40, 60, 80, 100, 120, 140 degrees (the ring No.1 for41614  1   18 
           seven assemblies) or at 0, 40, 60, 75, 91, 107, 125,   41614  1   19 
           150 degrees (the ring No. 2 for eight assemblies). In  41614  1   20 
           this arrangement, the neutron energy interval          41614  1   21 
           13.4 - 14.9 MeV was covered.                           41614  1   22 
           Most of the standard sample assemblies:                41614  1   23 
            Nb- sample X1 - Al - sample X2 -Nb or                 41614  1   24 
            Al -sample Y1 - Nb -sample Y2 -Al.                    41614  1   25 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) Variations of the neutron flux during           41614  1   26 
           irradiation were measured by two independent           41614  1   27 
           scintillation detectors.                               41614  1   28 
           (GELI) Ge(Li) detector of 160 cm3 volume, energy       41614  1   29 
           resolution 4.0keV at Egamma=1332.5 keV                 41614  1   30 
            and/or                                                41614  1   31 
           (HPGE) high-pure Ge detector with energy resolution    41614  1   32 
           1.8 keV at Egamma 1332.5 keV and relative efficiency   41614  1   33 
           24.7%                                                  41614  1   34 
            were used for measurement of gamma radiation of       41614  1   35 
           activated samples.                                     41614  1   36 
METHOD     (ACTIV)                                                41614  1   37 
           Contribution of scattered neutrons was minimized by the41614  1   38 
           use of thin-wall constructions of the target chamber   41614  1   39 
           and sample holders.                                    41614  1   40 
           The target warm was withdrawn with a focused air jet.  41614  1   41 
           The target-sample distance - 30 mm, beam diameter 5mm, 41614  1   42 
           diameter of the sample 14 mm, sample thickness ~1 mm.  41614  1   43 
ANALYSIS    All data were revised with the latest reference       41614  1   44 
           parameters: the reference cross-sections, isotopic     41614  1   45 
           abundance of the target nuclei, half-lives and gamma   41614  1   46 
           intensities of the reaction products.                  41614  1   47 
CORRECTION For backgrounds.                                       41614  1   48 
           For effect of gamma cascades.                          41614  1   49 
           For gamma coincidence.                                 41614  1   50 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total uncertainty.                             41614  1   51 
            Most important contributions from:                    41614  1   52 
           (ERR-1) Reference data uncertainty includes            41614  1   53 
           uncertainties of                                       41614  1   54 
           - the reference cross section 0.4-0.8 % ;              41614  1   55 
           - the target isotope abundance 0.01 - 7.5 % ;          41614  1   56 
           - the decay data 0.01 - 35. % ;                        41614  1   57 
           - correction factor responsible for the decay during   41614  1   58 
           irradiation, cooling and gamma counting.               41614  1   59 
           (ERR-2,1.,40.) area of gamma-peak - (1% - 40%);        41614  1   60 
           (ERR-3,1.2,1.5) efficiency of gamma-detector -         41614  1   61 
                      (1.2% - 1.5%);                              41614  1   62 
           (ERR-4,0.01,8.5) corrections for self-absorption and   41614  1   63 
           gamma-cascade summing - (0.01% - 8.5%);                41614  1   64 
           (ERR-6,0.01,0.1) sample mass - (0.01% - 0.1%);         41614  1   65 
           It's assumed that the uncertainty contributors are     41614  1   66 
           independent.                                           41614  1   67 
           The contribution of uncertainties of other parameters  41614  1   68 
           is small and can be neglected.                         41614  1   69
